# TODO — eskrev

## Concluído

### Corpus linguístico (src/assets/corpus/) — COMPLETO
- [x] Facade `src/js/modules/corpus.js` com lazy-load, cache, `_flatten()`, helpers especializados
- [x] morphology: classes, flexion_verbal, flexion_nominal, word_formation, prefixes, suffixes, roots
- [x] orthography: accentuation, spelling_rules, hyphen
- [x] punctuation: punctuation
- [x] syntax: sentence_analysis, concordancia, regencia (+ crase)
- [x] semantics: semantics
- [x] stylistics: figures
- [x] variation: linguistic_variation
- [x] text_production: text_genres, cohesion_coherence, argumentation
- [x] literature: literary_periods, literary_analysis
- 22 arquivos · 9 áreas · ~480KB · zero dependências

### RFC-0001 F1 (sessão anterior)
- [x] Estrutura Claude Code configurada
- [x] Testes automáticos passaram (check_uix_budget, check_dom_wiring, check_lang_*)
